declare_counter Rome_undersiege
set_counter Rome_undersiege 0
;monitor_event SettlementTurnStart SettlementName Roma
    ;and I_CompareCounter Rome_undersiege = 0
    ;if I_SettlementOwner Roma = romans_scipii
    ;and I_FactionBesieging roman_rebels
    ;set_counter Rome_undersiege 1
    ;end_if
;end_monitor
monitor_event SettlementTurnStart SettlementName Roma
if I_CompareCounter Rome_undersiege = 0
	and I_SettlementOwner Roma = romans_scipii
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage general, 2 95,127
		set_counter Rome_undersiege 1
	end_if
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage family, 2 95,127
		set_counter Rome_undersiege 1
	end_if
end_if
if I_CompareCounter Rome_undersiege = 2
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage family, 2 95,127
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage general, 2 95,127
	set_counter Rome_undersiege 0
end_if

monitor_event SettlementTurnEnd SettlementName Roma
and I_CompareCounter Rome_undersiege = 1
	if I_SettlementOwner Roma = romans_scipii
	and I_FactionBesieged romans_scipii
    and I_CompareCounter Rome_undersiege = 1
    and I_CompareCounter MarianLegions = 0
		console_command create_unit Roma "roman triarii" 4 1 1 1
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman princeps" 5 1 2 1
		console_command create_unit Roma "roman hastati" 5 1 2 1
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman hastati" 1 1 2 1
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman velite" 2 2 0 2
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman city militia" 2 3 3 3
        console_command add_money romans_scipii, 10000
        set_counter Rome_undersiege 2
end_if

	if I_SettlementOwner Roma = romans_scipii
	and I_FactionBesieged romans_scipii
    and I_CompareCounter Rome_undersiege = 1
    and I_CompareCounter MarianLegions = 1
		console_command create_unit Roma "roman republican legion" 5 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman republican legion" 5 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman republican legion" 5 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman velite" 2 0 2 2
		console_command create_unit Roma "roman archer" 2 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Roma "roman city militia" 1 3 3 3
        console_command add_money romans_scipii, 10000
        set_counter Roma_undersiege 2
end_if
end_monitor

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;roman mobilize;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
declare_counter roman_mobilize
set_counter roman_mobilize 0
monitor_event FactionTurnStart FactionType romans_scipii
and not FactionIsLocal
and I_NumberOfSettlements romans_scipii > 0
        if I_SettlementOwner Roma != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
	end_if
        if I_SettlementOwner Arretium != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
    end_if
        if I_SettlementOwner Ariminum != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
    end_if
        if I_SettlementOwner Capua != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
    end_if
        if I_SettlementOwner Croton != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
    end_if
        if I_SettlementOwner Tarentum != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
	end_if
		if I_SettlementOwner Ancona != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
	end_if
		if I_SettlementOwner Segesta != romans_scipii
        set_counter roman_mobilize 1
	end_if

if I_SettlementOwner Roma = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Arretium = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Ariminum = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Capua = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Croton = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Tarentum = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Ancona = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Segesta = romans_scipii
set_counter roman_mobilize 0
end_if 
end_monitor

declare_counter Burdigala_undersiege
set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 0

monitor_event FactionTurnEnd FactionType romans_scipii
if I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 0
	and I_SettlementOwner Burdigala = gauls
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii general, 2 44,150
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 1
	end_if
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii family, 2 44,150
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 1
	end_if
end_if
if I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 2
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii family, 2 44,150
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii general, 2 44,150
	set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 0
end_if
end_monitor

monitor_event FactionTurnEnd FactionType carthage
if I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 0
	and I_SettlementOwner Burdigala = gauls
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage general, 2 44,150
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 1
	end_if
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage family, 2 44,150
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 1
	end_if
end_if
if I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 2
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage family, 2 44,150
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage general, 2 44,150
	set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 0
end_if
end_monitor

monitor_event FactionTurnEnd FactionType germans
if I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 0
	and I_SettlementOwner Burdigala = gauls
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile germans general, 2 44,150
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 1
	end_if
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile germans family, 2 44,150
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 1
	end_if
end_if
if I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 2
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile germans family, 2 44,150
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile germans general, 2 44,150
	set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 0
end_if
end_monitor

and not SettlementIsLocal
and I_CompareCounter Burdigala_undersiege = 1

	and I_FactionBesieged gauls
		set_counter Burdigala_undersiege 2
        console_command create_unit Burdigala "barb naked fanatics gauls" 2 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Burdigala "heavy warband" 2 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Burdigala "warband sword gaul" 4 2 2 2

		console_command create_unit Burdigala "barb infantry gaul" 2 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Burdigala "gaul heavy cavlry" 2 0 2 2
end_if
end_monitor

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;Carthaginian revolt;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
declare_counter carthaginian_revolt
set_counter carthaginian_revolt 0
monitor_event FactionTurnStart FactionType carthage
    if I_CompareCounter carthaginian_revolt = 0
    and I_NumberOfSettlements carthage > 0
    and I_SettlementOwner Cirta != romans_scipii
    and I_SettlementOwner Carthago = romans_scipii
    and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage family, 2 82,101
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile carthage general, 2 82,101
    set_counter carthaginian_revolt 1
	end_if
	if I_CompareCounter carthaginian_revolt = 2
    and I_SettlementOwner Carthago = carthage

and not SettlementIsLocal
if I_CompareCounter Hadrumetum_undersiege = 0
	and I_SettlementOwner Hadrumetum = carthage
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii general, 2 85,95
		set_counter Hadrumetum_undersiege 1
	end_if
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii family, 2 85,95
		set_counter Hadrumetum_undersiege 1
	end_if
end_if

	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii family, 2 85,95
	and not I_CharacterTypeNearTile romans_scipii general, 2 85,95

		unit thracian thureos swordsmen, exp 2 armour 2 weapon_lvl 2
        unit thracian hoplite, exp 2 armour 2 weapon_lvl 2

        console_command create_unit Tanais "greek hoplite" 4 2 2 2
		console_command create_unit Tanais "thureos spears" 4 2 2 2
		console_command create_unit Tanais "greek swordsmen" 4 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Tanais "cimmerian hoplite elite" 4 1 2 2
        console_command create_unit Tanais "cimmerian thureos" 2 1 2 2

if I_NumberOfSettlements romans_julii < 6
    spawn_army

			character Androcles, general, age 30, x 175, y 155
			unit thureos spears, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit thureos spears, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2

            unit greek peltast, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 3
			unit greek swordsmen, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2

			unit greek swordsmen, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit greek swordsmen, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit heavy thureos swordsmen, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit heavy thureos swordsmen, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit heavy thureos swordsmen, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit cimmerian hoplite elite, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit cimmerian hoplite elite, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit thureos spears, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit thureos spears, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit cimmerian archer elite, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit cimmerian archer elite, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit cimmerian royal hippeis, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit cimmerian royal cavalry, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
			unit bosporan cataphract, exp 3 armour 3 weapon_lvl 2
end

    and I_CompareCounter Campus_Siracae_undersiege = 1
		set_counter Campus_Siracae_undersiege 2
		console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "scythian skirmisher" 2 1 1 1
        console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "barb archer scythian" 2 1 1 1
		console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "barb infantry scythia" 3 2 1 1
		console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "warband axe scythian" 4 1 1 1
        console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "warband swords scythian chosen" 2 1 1 1
        console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "barb horse archers scythian" 2 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "barb noble horse archers scythian" 1 0 2 2
        console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "barb scythian nobles" 2 0 1 2
        console_command create_unit Campus_Siracae "barb head hunting maidens scythian" 2 1 2 1
        
        console_command add_money scythia, 40000
        if I_NumberOfSettlements scythia < 5
        and I_FactionBesieged scythia
        console_command kill_character "Scylurus"
            spawn_army

			unit egyptian cleruch, exp 3 armour 1 weapon_lvl 1
            unit egyptian cleruch, exp 3 armour 1 weapon_lvl 1
			unit greek xystophoroi, exp 3 armour 1 weapon_lvl 1
			unit greek xystophoroi, exp 3 armour 1 weapon_lvl 1
			unit greek royal cavalry, exp 3 armour 1 weapon_lvl 1
            end        
end_if
set_counter Memphis_undersiege 2
end_if
end_monitor

        console_command create_unit Thebes "thureos swordsmen" 4 3 2 2
		console_command create_unit Thebes "thureos spears" 3 3 2 2
        console_command create_unit Thebes "greek pikemen" 3 2 2 2
		console_command create_unit Thebes "egyptian nile infantry" 2 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Thebes "egyptian cleruch" 2 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Thebes "egyptian infantry" 2 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Thebes "egyptian peltast" 2 3 2 3
		console_command create_unit Thebes "greek xystophoroi" 1 0 2 2
		console_command create_unit Thebes "greek royal cavalry" 1 0 2 2

console_command add_money egypt, 40000
set_counter Thebes_undersiege 2
end_if
end_monitor

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;Pontus_emergency;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

    and I_NumberOfSettlements pontus < 7
if I_CompareCounter Pontus_emergency = 0
	and I_SettlementOwner Amasia = pontus
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile egypt general, 2 175,157
        and I_FactionBesieged pontus
		set_counter Pontus_emergency 1
	end_if
	if I_CharacterTypeNearTile egypt family, 2 175,157
        and I_FactionBesieged pontus

	end_if

		set_counter Sinope_undersiege 2
        console_command create_unit Sinope "thureos swordsmen" 4 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Sinope "thureos spears" 4 2 2 2
        console_command create_unit Sinope "east heavy cavalry" 2 2 2 2
		console_command create_unit Sinope "east peltast" 1 2 2 2
		console_command create_unit Sinope "greek pikemen" 2 2 2 2
		console_command create_unit Sinope "east infantry" 2 2 2 2
end_if

and I_SettlementOwner Syracuse != romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Lilybaeum != romans_scipii

senate_mission_take_city moderate_reward, Syracuse
senate_mission_take_city moderate_reward, Lilybaeum

settlement_flash_start Syracuse
settlement_flash_start Lilybaeum

end_if

and I_SettlementOwner Messana = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Syracuse = romans_scipii
and I_SettlementOwner Lilybaeum = romans_scipii
settlement_flash_stop Lilybaeum
settlement_flash_stop Syracuse
settlement_flash_stop Messana

set_counter Sicily_conquering 0
end_if

and not SettlementBuildingExists = BATTLE_OF_PHILIPPI

and I_SettlementOwner Alexandria != romans_scipii

and I_SettlementOwner Alexandria = romans_scipii

end_if
